Structure & Module Organization\n`quantaalpha/` contains the Python package and core pipeline code. Key areas include `pipeline/` for mining and backtest entrypoints, `core/` for framework logic, `factors/` for factor generation utilities, and `backtest/` for standalone backtesting. Runtime configs live in `configs/`, generated outputs go to `data/results/` and `log/`, and longer-form docs live in `docs/`. The web UI is isolated in `frontend-v2/` with React sources under `frontend-v2/src/` and a small Python backend in `frontend-v2/backend/`.\n\n## Build, Test, and Development Commands\nInstall the Python package in editable mode with `SETUPTOOLS_SCM_PRETEND_VERSION=0.1.0 pip install -e .` and then `pip install -r requirements.txt`. Start the main workflow with `./run.sh \"Price-Volume Factor Mining\"` after copying `configs/.env.example` to `.env`. Use `python launcher.py mine --direction \"momentum reversal\"` for direct CLI access, or `python -m quantaalpha.backtest.run_backtest -c configs/backtest.yaml --factor-source custom --factor-json all_factors_library.json` for independent backtests. Build docs with `make -C docs html`. For the frontend, run `cd frontend-v2 && npm run dev`, `npm run build`, or `npm run lint`.\n\n## Coding Style & Naming Conventions\nFollow existing Python style: 4-space indentation, type hints where practical, snake_case for modules/functions, and PascalCase for classes. Keep imports grouped and formatted for `isort`; use `black` for formatting and `ruff` plus `mypy` for linting and static checks:\n`python -m black quantaalpha`\n`python -m isort quantaalpha`\n`python -m ruff check quantaalpha`\n`python -m mypy quantaalpha`\n\nIn `frontend-v2/src/`, prefer TypeScript function components, PascalCase component files, and camelCase hooks/state names.\n\n## Testing Guidelines\nPython test dependencies are listed in `requirements/test.txt` and use `pytest` with `coverage`. The repository does not currently ship a dedicated `tests/` tree, so new tests should be added under `tests/` or beside the module they exercise using `test_*.py` naming. Run `pytest` before opening a PR; use `coverage run -m pytest` when touching mining, backtest, or config-loading paths.\n\n## Commit & Pull Request Guidelines\nRecent history uses short, plain subjects (`first`, `first real shot`), but contributors should use clearer imperative messages such as `Add factor cache validation`. Keep commits focused and easy to review. PRs should summarize the behavioral change, list any config or data prerequisites, link related issues, and include screenshots for `frontend-v2` UI changes. Call out any `.env`, dataset, or backtest assumptions explicitly.\n\n## Security & Configuration Tips\nDo not commit `.env`, API keys, raw datasets, or generated logs. Keep large HDF5/Qlib inputs under ignored data directories such as `git_ignore_folder/` and verify `QLIB_DATA_DIR` and `DATA_RESULTS_DIR` before running experiments.\n\n</system-reminder>","title":"third_party/quantaalpha/quantaalpha/factors/library.py","metadata":{"preview":"\"\"\"\nFactor library manager: save experiment output to unified JSON factor library.\nCalled from quantaalpha/pipeline/loop.py feedback step.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport fcntl\nimport hashlib\nimport json\nimport logging\nimport os\nimport tempfile\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Any, Optional\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport pandas as pd\n\nfrom quantaalpha.factors.status_rules import update_factor_status\n","truncated":false,"loaded":["/home/quan/testdata/aspipe_v4/third_party/quantaalpha/AGENTS.md"]},"time":{"start":1773912578115,"end":1773912578127}}}}

_sync_h5_to_md5_cache(\n        factor_expression: str, h5_path: str, cache_dir: Optional[str] = None\n    ) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Sync factor values from result.h5 to MD5 cache dir (.pkl). Returns True on success.\"\"\"\n        cache_dir = Path(cache_dir or DEFAULT_FACTOR_CACHE_DIR)\n        h5_file = Path(h5_path)\n\n        if not h5_file.exists():\n            return False\n\n        md5_key = hashlib.md5(factor_expression.encode()).hexdigest()\n        pkl_file = cache_dir / f\"{md5_key}.pkl\"\n\n        if pkl_file.exists():\n            return True\n\n        try:\n            cache_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n            result = pd.read_hdf(str(h5_file))\n            result.to_pickle(pkl_file)\n            logger.debug(f\"Synced factor cache -> {pkl_file.name}\")\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.debug(f\"Sync factor cache failed [{h5_path}]: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def check_cache_status(library_path: str, cache_dir: Optional[str] = None) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Check cache status for each factor in library. Returns:\n        {\n            \"total\": int,\n            \"h5_cached\": int,\n            \"md5_cached\": int,\n            \"need_compute\": int,\n            \"factors\": [ { \"factor_id\", \"factor_name\", \"status\" }, ... ]\n        }\n        \"\"\"\n        cache_dir = Path(cache_dir or DEFAULT_FACTOR_CACHE_DIR)\n\n        with open(library_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            data = json.load(f)\n\n        factors = data.get(\"factors\", {})\n        total = len(factors)\n        h5_cached = 0\n        md5_cached = 0\n        need_compute = 0\n        details = []\n\n        for fid, finfo in factors.items():\n            expr = finfo.get(\"factor_expression\", \"\")\n            cloc = finfo.get(\"cache_location\", {})\n            h5_path = cloc.get(\"result_h5_path\", \"\")\n\n            status = \"need_compute\"\n            # Check h5 cache\n            if h5_path and Path(h5_path).exists():\n                status = \"h5_cached\"\n                h5_cached += 1\n            # Check MD5 cache\n            elif expr:\n                md5_key = hashlib.md5(expr.encode()).hexdigest()\n                if (cache_dir / f\"{md5_key}.pkl\").exists():\n                    status = \"md5_cached\"\n                    md5_cached += 1\n\n            if status == \"need_compute\":\n                need_compute += 1\n\n            details.append(\n                {\n                    \"factor_id\": fid,\n                    \"factor_name\": finfo.get(\"factor_name\", fid),\n                    \"status\": status,\n                }\n            )\n\n        return {\n            \"total\": total,\n            \"h5_cached\": h5_cached,\n            \"md5_cached\": md5_cached,\n            \"need_compute\": need_compute,\n            \"factors\": details,\n        }\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def warm_cache_from_json(\n        library_path: str, cache_dir: Optional[str] = None\n    ) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Walk factor library JSON and sync all available result.h5 to MD5 cache dir. Returns:\n        { \"total\": int, \"synced\": int, \"skipped\": int, \"failed\": int,\n          \"already_cached\": int, \"no_source\": int }\n        \"\"\"\n        cache_dir_path = Path(cache_dir or DEFAULT_FACTOR_CACHE_DIR)\n\n        with open(library_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            data = json.load(f)\n\n        factors = data.get(\"factors\", {})\n        synced = 0\n        skipped = 0\n        failed = 0\n        already_cached = 0\n        no_source = 0\n\n        for fid, finfo in factors.items():\n            expr = finfo.get(\"factor_expression\", \"\")\n            cloc = finfo.get(\"cache_location\", {})\n            h5_path = cloc.get(\"result_h5_path\", \"\")\n\n            if not expr or not h5_path:\n                no_source += 1\n                skipped += 1\n                continue\n\n            md5_key = hashlib.md5(expr.encode()).hexdigest()\n            pkl_file = cache_dir_path / f\"{md5_key}.pkl\"\n\n            if pkl_file.exists():\n                already_cached += 1\n                skipped += 1\n                continue\n\n            if not Path(h5_path).exists():\n                failed += 1\n                continue\n\n            try:\n                cache_dir_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n                result = pd.read_hdf(str(h5_path))\n                result.to_pickle(pkl_file)\n                synced += 1\n            except Exception:\n                failed += 1\n\n        return {\n            \"total\": len(factors),\n            \"synced\": synced,\n            \"skipped\": skipped,\n            \"failed\": failed,\n            \"already_cached\": already_cached,\n            \"no_source\": no_source,\n        }\n\n    def _normalize_library_data(self, data: dict) -> dict:\n        data = data or {}\n        metadata = data.setdefault(\"metadata\", {})\n        metadata.setdefault(\"created_at\", datetime.now().isoformat())\n        metadata.setdefault(\"last_updated\", datetime.now().isoformat())\n        metadata[\"version\"] = \"1.1\"\n        data.setdefault(\"factors\", {})\n        data.setdefault(\"audit_log\", [])\n        normalized_factors = {}\n        for factor_id, factor_entry in data[\"factors\"].items():\n            normalized = self._normalize_factor_entry(factor_entry)\n            normalized_factors[normalized.get(\"factor_id\", factor_id)] = normalized\n        data[\"factors\"] = normalized_factors\n        metadata[\"total_factors\"] = len(normalized_factors)\n        return data\n\n    def get_library_summary(self) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get summary statistics for the factor library.\n\n        Returns:\n            Dict with:\n                - total_factors: int\n                - active_count: int\n                - stale_count: int\n                - degraded_count: int\n                - pending_validation_count: int\n                - deprecated_count: int\n                - status_distribution: dict[str, int]\n                - last_updated: str | None\n                - last_validated: str | None\n        \"\"\"\n        factors = self.data.get(\"factors\", {})\n        status_counts: dict[str, int] = {}\n        last_validated: Optional[str] = None\n\n        for fid, fdata in factors.items():\n            status = fdata.get(\"evaluation\", {}).get(\"status\", \"pending_validation\")\n            status_counts[status] = status_counts.get(status, 0) + 1\n\n            # Track most recent validation\n            lv = fdata.get(\"evaluation\", {}).get(\"last_validated\")\n            if lv:\n                if last_validated is None or lv > last_validated:\n                    last_validated = lv\n\n        return {\n            \"total_factors\": len(factors),\n            \"active_count\": status_counts.get(\"active\", 0),\n            \"stale_count\": status_counts.get(\"stale\", 0),\n            \"degraded_count\": status_counts.get(\"degraded\", 0),\n            \"pending_validation_count\": status_counts.get(\"pending_validation\", 0),\n            \"deprecated_count\": status_counts.get(\"deprecated\", 0),\n            \"status_distribution\": status_counts,\n            \"last_updated\": self.data.get(\"metadata\", {}).get(\"last_updated\"),\n            \"last_validated\": last_validated,\n        }\n\n    def get_audit_log(self, limit: Optional[int] = None) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Get audit log entries, most recent first.\n\n        Args:\n            limit: Maximum number of entries to return. None returns all.\n\n        Returns:\n            List of audit records, each with:\n                - timestamp: str\n                - factor_id: str\n                - old_status: str\n                - new_status: str\n                - trigger: str\n        \"\"\"\n        audit_log = self.data.get(\"audit_log\", [])\n        # Already sorted most recent first (we append to front)\n        if limit is not None:\n            return audit_log[:limit]\n        return list(audit_log)\n\n    def _append_audit_record(\n        self,\n        factor_id: str,\n        old_status: str,\n        new_status: str,\n        trigger: str = \"unknown\",\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Append an audit record for status change.\"\"\"\n        if old_status == new_status:\n            return  # No audit for same status\n\n        record = {\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.now().isoformat(),\n            \"factor_id\": factor_id,\n            \"old_status\": old_status,\n            \"new_status\": new_status,\n            \"trigger\": trigger,\n        }\n\n        # Initialize audit_log if not present\n        if \"audit_log\" not in self.data:\n            self.data[\"audit_log\"] = []\n\n        # Prepend (most recent first)\n        self.data[\"audit_log\"].insert(0, record)\n\n        # Trim to max records\n        if len(self.data[\"audit_log\"]) > MAX_AUDIT_RECORDS:\n            self.data[\"audit_log\"] = self.data[\"audit_log\"][:MAX_AUDIT_RECORDS]\n\n    def _normalize_factor_entry(self, factor_entry: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        entry = dict(factor_entry or {})\n        entry.setdefault(\"factor_id\", \"\")\n        entry.setdefault(\"factor_name\", \"\")\n        entry.setdefault(\"factor_expression\", \"\")\n        entry.setdefault(\"metadata\", {})\n        entry.setdefault(\"backtest_results\", {})\n        entry.setdefault(\"feedback\", {})\n        entry[\"metadata\"].setdefault(\"version\", \"1.1\")\n entry[\"evaluation\"].setdefault(\"status\", \"pending_validation\")\n        entry[\"evaluation\"].setdefault(\"last_validated\", None)\n        entry[\"evaluation\"].setdefault(\"stability_score\", None)\n        entry[\"evaluation\"].setdefault(\"period_results\", [])\n        entry[\"evaluation\"].setdefault(\"validation_summary\", \"\")\n self,\n        factor_entry: dict[str, Any],\n        validation_result: dict[str, Any],\n        *,\n        now: Optional[datetime] = None,\n        config: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,\n        persist: bool = True,\n        trigger: str = \"unknown\",\n    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Apply validation result to factor entry and optionally persist.\n\n        Args:\n            factor_entry: Factor data to update\n            validation_result: Validation result dict with status, period_results, summary\n            now: Current timestamp (for testing)\n            config: Status transition config\n            persist: Whether to save to disk\n            trigger: Trigger source for audit log (e.g., 'real_backtest', 'revalidate_cli')\n\n        Returns:\n            Updated factor entry\n        \"\"\"\n        old_status = factor_entry.get(\"evaluation\", {}).get(\"status\", \"pending_validation\")\n\n        updated = update_factor_status(\n            factor_entry=factor_entry,\n            validation_result=validation_result,\n            now=now,\n            config=config,\n        )\n\n        new_status = updated.get(\"evaluation\", {}).get(\"status\", \"pending_validation\")\n        factor_id = updated.get(\"factor_id\", \"\")\n\n        # Record audit if status changed\n        if old_status != new_status:\n Optional[datetime] = None,\n    ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:\n        selected = []\n        now = now or datetime.now()\n        factor_id_set = {\n            fid.strip() for fid in (factor_ids or [])       validated_at = datetime.fromisoformat(str(last_validated))\n                    except ValueError:\n                        validated_at = now - timedelta(days=days + 1)\n                    if (now - validated_at).days < days:\n                        continue\n            selected.append(entry)\n        return selected\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _infer_dimensions(factor_entry: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:\n        expr = str(factor_entry.get(\"factor_expression\", \"\"))\n        dimensions = [\"price_volume\"]\n        if any(token in expr.lower() for token in (\"roe\", \"roa\", \"profit\", \"margin\")):\n            dimensions.append(\"financial\")\n        return dimensions\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _infer_fields(factor_entry: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:\n        expr       \"$volume\",\n            \"$amount\",\n            \"$roe\",\n            \"$roa\",\n            \"$net_profit_margin\",\n        ):\n            if token.lower() in expr.lower():\n                fields.append(token)\n        return fields\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _extract_backtest_results(experiment) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Extract backtest metrics from experiment.result (pandas Series) as dict.\"\"\"\n        result = getattr(experiment, \"result\", None)\n        if result is None:\n            return {}\n        if isinstance(result, pd.Series):\n            out = {}\n            for key, val in result.items():\n                # NaN/Inf -> None for JSON\n                if isinstance(val, (float, np.floating)):\n                    if np.isnan(val) or np.isinf(val):\n                        out[str(key)] = None\n                    else:\n                        out[str(key)] = round(float(val), 8)\n                else:\n                    out[str(key)] = val\n            return out\n\n        if isinstance(result, pd.DataFrame):\n            try:\n                return {\n                    str(k): round(float(v), 8)\n                    if isinstance(v, (float, np.floating)) and not np.isnan(v)\n                    else None\n                    for k, v in result.iloc[:, 0].items()\n                }\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n\n        if isinstance(result, dict):\n            return result\n\n        return {}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _extract_feedback(feedback) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Convert feedback object to serializable dict.\"\"\"\n        if feedback is None:\n            return {}\n        if isinstance(feedback, dict):\n            return feedback\n\n        out = {}\n        for attr in [\n            \"observations\",\n            \"hypothesis_evaluation\",\n            \"decision\",\n            \"reason\",\n            \"new_hypothesis\",\n            \"feedback_str\",\n        ]:\n            val = getattr(feedback, attr, None)\n            if val is not None:\n                out[attr] = str(val) if not isinstance(val, (bool, int, float)) else val\n        if not out:\n \"data/factorlib/all_factors_library.json\"\nMAX_AUDIT_RECORDS = 1000\n\n\nclass FactorLibraryManager:\n    \"\"\"Manage unified factor library (CRUD).\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, library_path: str):\n        self.library_path = Path(library_path)\n        self.data = self._load()\n\n    def _load(self) -> dict:\n        if self.library_path.exists():\n            try:\n                with open(self.library_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                    data = json.load(f)\n                    return self._normalize_library_data(data)\n            except (json.JSONDecodeError, Exception) as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Factor library file corrupted, recreating: {e}\")\n        return self._normalize_library_data(\n            {\n                \"metadata\": {\n                    \"created_at\": datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                    \"last_updated\": datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                    \"total_factors\": 0,\n                    \"version\": \"1.1\",\n                },\n                \"factors\": {},\n            }\n        )\n\n    def _save(self, timeout: float = 30.0):\n        \"\"\"Save library data with file locking and atomic write.\n\n        Args:\n            timeout: Maximum time to wait for lock acquisition (seconds).\n                     Set to 0 for non-blocking (raises TimeoutError if lock held).\n\n        Raises:\n            TimeoutError: If lock cannot be acquired within timeout.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.data[\"metadata\"][\"last_updated\"] = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.data[\"metadata\"][\"total_factors\"] = len(self.data[\"factors\"])\n        self.data[\"metadata\"][\"version\"] = \"1.1\"\n        self.library_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n        lock_path = str(self.library_path) + \".lock\"\n\n        # Acquire file lock\n        with open(lock_path, \"w\") as lock_file:\n            try:\n                # Set lock flags based on timeout\n                if timeout == 0:\n                    # Non-blocking\n                    fcntl.flock(lock_file.fileno(), fcntl.LOCK_EX | fcntl.LOCK_NB)\n                else:\n                    # Blocking with implicit timeout from OS\n                    fcntl.flock(lock_file.fileno(), fcntl.LOCK_EX)\n            except BlockingIOError:\n                raise TimeoutError(f\"Could not acquire lock on {lock_path}\")\n\n            try:\n                # Reload to merge with any changes made by other processes\n                if self.library_path.exists():\n                    try:\n                        with open(self.library_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                            file_data = json.load(f)\n                        # Merge: prefer in-memory data for factors we have\n                        file_factors = file_data.get(\"factors\", {})\n                        for fid, fdata in file_factors.items():\n                            if fid not in self.data[\"factors\"]:\n                                self.data[\"factors\"][fid] = fdata\n                        # Preserve audit_log from file if we haven't modified it\n                        if \"audit_log\" in file_data and len(\n                            file_data[\"audit_log\"]\n                        ) > len(self.data.get(\"audit_log\", [])):\n                            self.data[\"audit_log\"] = file_data[\"audit_log\"]\n                    except (json.JSONDecodeError, Exception):\n                        pass  # Use in-memory data\n\n                # Atomic write: write to temp file, then replace\n                with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(\n                    mode=\"w\",\n                    encoding=\"utf-8\",\n                    dir=str(self.library_path.parent),\n                    prefix=str(self.library_path.name) + \".tmp_\",\n                    delete=False,\n                ) as tmp_file:\n                    json.dump(\n                        self.data, tmp_file, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2, default=str\n                    )\n                    tmp_path = fcntl.LOCK_UN)\n\n    def add_factors_from_experiment(\n        self,\n        experiment,\n        experiment_id: str = \"unknown\",\n        round_number: int = 0,\n        hypothesis: Optional[str] getattr(experiment, \"sub_workspace_list\", []) or []\n\n        for idx, task in enumerate(sub_tasks):\n            factor_name = getattr(\n                task, \"factor_name\", getattr(task, f\"{factor_name}_{factor_expr}\".encode()\n            ).hexdigest()[:16]\n\n            code = \"\"\n            cache_location = {}\n            if idx < len(sub_workspaces):\n                ws = \"backtest_results\": backtest_results,\n                \"feedback\": feedback_dict,\n            }\n            factor_entry = self._normalize_factor_entry(factor_entry)\n\n      )\n\n            self.data[\"factors\"][factor_id] = factor_entry\n\n            if factor_expr and cache_location.get(\"result_h5_path\"):\n                self._sync_h5_to_md5_cache(\n                    factor_expr, cache_location[\"result_h5_path\"]\n                )\n\n        self._save()\n        logger.info(\n            f\"Saved {len(sub_tasks)} factors to {self.library_path}  ) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Sync factor values from result.h5 to MD5 cache dir (.pkl). Returns True on success.\"\"\"\n        cache_dir = Path(cache_dir or DEFAULT_FACTOR_CACHE_DIR)\n        h5_file = Path(h5_path)\n\n        if not h5_file.exists():\n            return False\n\n        md5_key = hashlib.md5(factor_expression.encode()).hexdigest()\n        pkl_file = cache_dir / f\"{md5_key}.pkl\"\n\n        if pkl_file.exists():\n            return True\n\n        try:\n            cache_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n            result = pd.read_hdf(str(h5_file))\n            result.to_pickle(pkl_file)\n            logger.debug(f\"Synced factor cache -> {pkl_file.name}\")\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.debug(f\"Sync factor cache failed [{h5_path}]: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def check_cache_status(library_path: str, cache_dir: Optional[str] = None) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Check cache status for each factor in library.
